G-YON PAR BCING BAR BYA'O, ,DE NAS DE'I SNYING

@50A *, ,KHAR LAG PAS GTUGS TE SPYAN GYI SNGAGS LAN BRGYA BZLA
BAR BYA'O, ,GZHAN DAG LA NI JI SKAD DU BSHAD PA'I SBYIN SREG LAN
BDUN BDUN BYA'O, ,DE NAS BSANG GTOR DANG SRUNG SKUD BCING BA DANG
SNYING GAR GTUGS PA DAG KYANG BYA'O, ,RDO RJE SEMS SOGS SEMS DPA'

MCHOG; ,DNGOS GRUB THAMS CAD STZOL MDZAD PA, ,RDO RJE THAMS CAD
'BYUNG BYAS LAS, ,BDAG GIS DGE BA GANG BSAGS PA, ,DES NI 'JIG
RTEN MA LUS PA, ,KUN DGA' SNYING PO RIG PA MCHOG ,SEMS CAN KUN
GYI GNYEN GCIG PO, ,GTZO CHEN RDO RJE 'DZIN GYUR CIG,

DPAL DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA THAMS CAD KYI DE KHO NA NYID BSDUS PA,
THEG PA CHEN PO MNGON PAR RTOGS PA'I RGYUD CHEN PO LAS BTUS THAMS
CAD 'BYUNG BA ZHES BYA BA, RDO RJE SLOB DPON CHEN PO KUN THAMS
CAD 'BYUNG BA ZHES BYA BA, RDO RJE SLOB DPON CHEN PO KUN DGA'
SNYING PO'I ZHAL SNGA

NAS KYIS MDZAD PA RDZOGS SO,, ,,RGYA GAR GYI MKHAN PO A'A TZ'ARYA
BUDDHA SHR'I SH'ANTI DANG, ZHU CHEN GYI LO TZ'A BA DGE SLONG RIN
